  • Maybe in reply to: Mikael Nykvist: "Milo problems."
> So, what did I want with this mail?
>
> * Why does the x86 emulator in arc-srm/milo differ?

The latest sources include the latest BIOS emulation code. The latest sources
on gatekeeper are milo-2.0.22 but these also build against linux-2.0.23 as well
as linux-2.0.22.

> * Why can't you compile milo as elf? (Tons of stuff about 'relocation
> failed' when it tries to link it, we had to compile it as ecoff
> (ofcourse we recompiled davids free 86 emulator as elf, so we are not
> trying to link togheter with ecoff libs or anything stupid like that.)

See the uuencoded patch file at the end of the mail. This will be posted on
gatekeeper tonight. Note that when you build on ELF you cannot link in the
BIOS emulation but that does give you the freedom to do whatever you want.
You may still see a few errors , MILO's 'make clean' does not clean out
all of the libraries and so you will have to do some bits by hand.

> * Does any1 have an idea of a "better way" to do it (Hopefully ditch arc
> if possible..)?

A better way is always to blow MILO into flash, trouble is that that is not
supported on all systems.

> * Any chance of getting 'reboot' to work when you boot arc->milo->linux ?
>

I found a bug whereby 'shutdown -r now' didn't work. This is fixed in
the milo-2.0.23 sources that will go on gatekeeper tonight.

----------
